# Compliance Audit: Envoy Access Logging Configuration Coverage

## Your Task

Audit the access logging infrastructure in `envoyproxy/envoy`. Find all C++ source files under `source/extensions/access_loggers/` and `source/common/access_log/` that define access log filter implementations or access log sink implementations. Also find the corresponding `.proto` definitions in `envoyproxy/data-plane-api` under `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/`. For each implementation, report whether it supports structured (JSON) logging or only unstructured text logging.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the compliance domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2, sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367, sg-evals/go-control-plane--71637ad6, sg-evals/grpc--957dba5e.

## Findings Summary

### C++ Source Files (envoy--v1.31.2)

**`source/common/access_log/`** — Core filter and file management:
- `access_log_impl.h/.cc` — All built-in filter implementations: `StatusCodeFilter`, `DurationFilter`, `AndFilter`, `OrFilter`, `NotHealthCheckFilter`, `TraceableRequestFilter`, `RuntimeFilter`, `HeaderFilter`, `ResponseFlagFilter`, `GrpcStatusFilter`, `LogTypeFilter`, `MetadataFilter`, plus `FilterFactory` and `AccessLogFactory`
- `access_log_manager_impl.h/.cc` — `AccessLogManagerImpl` and `AccessLogFileImpl` (buffered file writer)

Infrastructure Audit\\n\\n### Overview\\n\\nThe access logging infrastructure in envoy--v1.31.2 is organized into two main areas:\\n1. `source/common/access_log/` \u2014 core filter logic and file management\\n2. `source/extensions/access_loggers/` \u2014 concrete sink implementations and extension filters\\n\\nCorresponding proto definitions live in `data-plane-api--84e84367/envoy/extensions/access_loggers/`.\\n\\n---\\n\\n### source/common/access_log/ \u2014 Core Filter Implementations\\n\\n**access_log_impl.h / access_log_impl.cc**\\nDefines all built-in access log *filter* implementations (not sinks). These filters decide whether a log entry should be emitted:\\n- `FilterFactory` \u2014 reads filter config from proto and instantiates the correct filter\\n- `ComparisonFilter` \u2014 base for numeric comparison filters\\n- `StatusCodeFilter` \u2014 filters on HTTP response status code\\n- `DurationFilter` \u2014 filters on request/response duration\\n- `OperatorFilter` \u2014 base for logical operator filters\\n- `AndFilter` \u2014 logical AND of sub-filters\\n- `OrFilter` \u2014 logical OR of sub-filters\\n- `NotHealthCheckFilter` \u2014 excludes health check requests\\n- `TraceableRequestFilter` \u2014 passes only traced requests\\n- `RuntimeFilter` \u2014 uses a runtime feature key for sampling\\n- `HeaderFilter` \u2014 filters based on request headers\\n- `ResponseFlagFilter` \u2014 filters on Envoy response flags\\n- `GrpcStatusFilter` \u2014 filters on gRPC status codes\\n- `LogTypeFilter` \u2014 filters on access log type (TCP/HTTP/etc.)\\n- `MetadataFilter` \u2014 filters based on dynamic metadata\\n- `AccessLogFactory` \u2014 instantiates access log sink instances from proto config\\n\\n**access_log_manager_impl.h / access_log_manager_impl.cc**\\nProvides the file-level sink infrastructure:\\n- `AccessLogManagerImpl` \u2014 manages a pool of open log files, creates `AccessLogFileImpl` instances\\n- `AccessLogFileImpl` \u2014 buffered, thread-safe file writer with a dedicated flush thread; used by all file-based sinks (file, stdout, stderr)\\n\\n---\\n\\n### source/extensions/access_loggers/ \u2014 Sink Implementations\\n\\n#### Common Infrastructure\\n\\n**common/access_log_base.h / .cc**\\n- `ImplBase` \u2014 abstract base class for all access log sink instances; applies the filter before calling `emitLog()`\\n\\n**common/file_access_log_impl.h / .cc**\\n- `FileAccessLog` \u2014 concrete sink that writes formatted log strings to a file (or stdout/stderr). Supports both unstructured text and structured JSON output depending on the `Formatter::FormatterPtr` it is given.\\n\\n**common/stream_access_log_common_impl.h**\\n- `createStreamAccessLogInstance<T, DestinationType>` \u2014 template factory used by stdout/stderr configs to create `FileAccessLog` instances targeting the appropriate stream.\\n\\n**common/grpc_access_logger.h**\\n- `GrpcAccessLogger<HttpLogProto, TcpLogProto, LogRequest, LogResponse>` \u2014 template base class for gRPC-based loggers; handles buffering, batching, and flushing over a gRPC stream or unary call.\\n- `GrpcAccessLoggerCache<GrpcAccessLogger, ConfigProto>` \u2014 thread-local cache of logger instances keyed by config hash.\\n\\n**common/grpc_access_logger_clients.h**\\n- `GrpcAccessLogClient<LogRequest, LogResponse>` \u2014 abstract gRPC client interface\\n- `UnaryGrpcAccessLogClient` \u2014 sends each batch as a unary gRPC request (used by OpenTelemetry)\\n- `StreamingGrpcAccessLogClient` \u2014 maintains a persistent gRPC stream (used by HTTP/TCP gRPC ALS)\\n\\n**common/grpc_access_logger_utils.h / .cc**\\n- `optionalRetryPolicy()` \u2014 helper to extract optional retry policy from gRPC config\\n\\n---\\n\\n#### File Access Logger (`envoy.access_loggers.file`)\\n\\n**file/config.h / config.cc** \u2014 `FileAccessLogFactory`\\n- **Supports BOTH structured (JSON) and unstructured (text) logging.**\\n- Accepts `format` (plain text string, deprecated), `json_format` (JSON dict, deprecated), `typed_json_format` (typed JSON dict, deprecated), and `log_format` (`SubstitutionFormatString`, which can be text or JSON).\\n- Proto: `data-plane-api--84e84367/envoy/extensions/access_loggers/file/v3/file.proto` \u2014 `FileAccessLog`\\n\\n---\\n\\n#### Stream Access Loggers (`envoy.access_loggers.stdout`, `envoy.access_loggers.stderr`)\\n\\n**stream/config.h / config.cc** \u2014 `StdoutAccessLogFactory`, `StderrAccessLogFactory`\\n- **Supports BOTH structured (JSON) and unstructured (text) logging** via `SubstitutionFormatString`.\\n- Both factories create `FileAccessLog` instances targeting `Filesystem::DestinationType::Stdout` or `Stderr`.\\n- Proto: `data-plane-api--84e84367/envoy/extensions/access_loggers/stream/v3/stream.proto` \u2014 `StdoutAccessLog`, `StderrAccessLog`\\n\\n---\\n\\n#### gRPC Access Log Service (ALS) \u2014 HTTP (`envoy.access_loggers.http_grpc`)\\n\\n**grpc/http_grpc_access_log_impl.h / .cc** \u2014 `HttpGrpcAccessLog`\\n- **Structured only** \u2014 emits `envoy.data.accesslog.v3.HTTPAccessLogEntry` protobuf messages over a gRPC streaming connection to an ALS server. No text/JSON formatting.\\n- Uses `GrpcAccessLoggerImpl` (grpc/grpc_access_log_impl.h) which wraps `StreamingGrpcAccessLogClient`.\\n\\n**grpc/http_config.h / http_config.cc** \u2014 `HttpGrpcAccessLogFactory`\\n\\n**grpc/grpc_access_log_impl.h / .cc** \u2014 `GrpcAccessLoggerImpl`, `GrpcAccessLoggerCacheImpl`\\n- Concrete gRPC logger for both HTTP and TCP ALS; batches entries into `StreamAccessLogsMessage`.\\n\\n**grpc/grpc_access_log_utils.h / .cc** \u2014 `Utility`\\n- `extractCommonAccessLogProperties()` \u2014 populates `AccessLogCommon` proto from stream info\\n- `responseFlagsToAccessLogResponseFlags()` \u2014 maps Envoy response flags to proto enum\\n\\n**grpc/grpc_access_log_proto_descriptors.h / .cc** \u2014 `validateProtoDescriptors()`\\n**grpc/config_utils.h / config_utils.cc** \u2014 `getGrpcAccessLoggerCacheSingleton()`\\n\\n- Proto: `data-plane-api--84e84367/envoy/extensions/access_loggers/grpc/v3/als.proto` \u2014 `HttpGrpcAccessLogConfig`, `CommonGrpcAccessLogConfig`\\n\\n---\\n\\n#### gRPC Access Log Service (ALS) \u2014 TCP (`envoy.access_loggers.tcp_grpc`)\\n\\n**grpc/tcp_grpc_access_log_impl.h / .cc** \u2014 `TcpGrpcAccessLog`\\n- **Structured only** \u2014 emits `envoy.data.accesslog.v3.TCPAccessLogEntry` protobuf messages over gRPC streaming.
